Subject: Application Feedback
From: "Wood, Thomas J" <thomas-wood@uiowa.edu>
Date: Sun, 16 Oct 2011 04:22:58 +0100
To: LHSee <lhsee@physics.ox.ac.uk>

*** Please send this email message as it is currently formatted. Thanks! ***
<answerForm>
<q1>Very interested.</q1>
<q2>Agree</q2>
<q3>Agree</q3>
<q4>Agree</q4>
<q5>22-35 years old.</q5>
<q6>A-Level / Advanced Higher.</q6>
<other>The list of options when identifying reactions truncates the reaction. This doesn't really hurt most of them, but since the tutorial never really goes over the expected Higgs boson decay products and the products are truncated to "...", the user is forced to simply pick Higgs boson when they see something unfamiliar, without really understanding what is going on.

Also, the app should remember (and have a reset option for) the progress through identifying the example decay spectra. I personally only had time to do one or two at any given time, and found it frustrating having to keep going through them trying to remember my place.

Also, the 3D display doesn't seem to show the same information as the 2D display? I don't recall if I ever saw muon paths plotted on a 3D display, and definitely never saw the missing-momentum lines on a 3D plot.

Overall I'd say this is an excellent app. It would be nice if there were a bit more to do after identifying the examples, other than just watch data go by. From the perspective of a chemistry grad student though, this app was a blast. All of my friends and coworkers who have seen it seem to also be impressed at a live LHC feed.</other>
<loc>US</loc>

</answerForm>
